Hong Kong Interport Football Team Arrives in Shanghai 200

= The entire team of sixteen people arrived here yesterday afternoon =

= Mo Yingwei led the team to create new rules for Hong Kong =

= There are six Chinese team members including Sun Jinshun =

Mo Yingwei talks about the recent situation of Guangdong-Hong Kong football

Hong Kong Inter-Port Football Team's First Chinese Leader, Mr. Mo Ying-kui (Photo by Li Zun-yong) 201

The Hong Kong Inter-Port Football Team, led by the Chinese Mr. Mo Ying-kui, arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the President McKinley of the Dollar Steamship Lines. At noon, they disembarked at the new customs wharf. They were greeted by a large crowd, including Mr. Hamson, secretary of the Western Football Club, Xu, captain of the Shanghai Inter-Port Team, reporters from various newspapers, and over a hundred football fans, who gathered around the wharf eager to catch a glimpse of their style. Their deep infatuation is evident.

〓 Team Appearance 〓

The Hong Kong team consists of sixteen people: leader Ying-kui, manager Holland, captain and goalkeeper Roger (Hong Kong Football Club), left back Muir (Welsh), right back Sturridge (Hong Kong Football Club), center back Pido (Artillery Team), left midfielder Duncan (Hong Kong Football Club), right midfielder Baleis (Kowloon Football Club), center forward Howie (Hong Kong Football Club), left inside forward Wong Mei-shun (South China), right inside forward Sun Kam-shun (China), left winger Bardley (Lincoln), right winger Zheng Shao-kang (South China), reserves: defender Liu Mao (South China), center back Liang Rong-zhao (South China), forward Balayan (Artillery Team). They are staying at the Palace Hotel on the Bund, Nanjing Road.

〓 Afternoon Practice 〓

After a short rest, at 3:00 PM, they went to the Racecourse football field for practice, a light warm-up to relieve the fatigue of the three-day sea journey. Photography reporters rushed to take photos of them. The five forwards' movements were remarkable. Zheng Shao-kang, Sun Kam-shun, and Wong Mei-shun were among them, along with center forward Howie and left winger Bardley. Their strength is not weak. No particular performance was seen from the defenders, so no judgment can be made.

〓 Mr. Mo's Remarks 〓

The reporter had a conversation with Mr. Mo Ying-kui, the first Chinese leader of the Hong Kong team. Mr. Mo is the chairman of the Hong Kong Chinese Sports Advancement Association. He spoke about the recent situation of the Hong Kong-Guangdong football scene and the selection process for this Hong Kong team. The record is as follows:

The Strength of the Hong Kong Team: The Hong Kong team's strength is in the forwards, which are good, with the three generals Sun, Wong, and Zheng, and Howie and Balayan being especially excellent. However, the defenders are somewhat inferior. No Chinese players were selected. If one or two generals from South China could be added, they would be stronger.

Selection Not Fully Satisfactory: The Hong Kong side expressed dissatisfaction with the selected team members. In the first friendly match, the intended team lost 3-0 to the Sino-Western United Team. In the second match, they lost 4-2 to the All-Chinese Team. Poor cooperation is the biggest reason. For example, Wong Mei-shun is a center back talent, but now he is being used as a left inside forward, which may not be suitable. There are also talented defenders in South China and China, but it is a pity that they could not be selected. I (Mr. Mo referring to himself) am the only Chinese selection committee member, so I am powerless.

Recent Situation of Hong Kong Football: South China and China have excellent results in the Hong Kong League. South China has only lost two points, so they have a good chance of winning the league. Since the split between the Chinese Sports Association and the Hong Kong Football Club last year and their withdrawal, they have reached a compromise again this year. The Hong Kong Football Club has begun to have a considerable understanding of the Association.

Preparing to Win the Governor's Cup: The Sports Association and the Hong Kong Football Club, in order to promote communication, have initiated the Governor's Cup competition this year. The Association team is the All-Chinese Team, and the Hong Kong Football Club team is the Western team. The winner is the one who wins two out of three matches. The first match is scheduled for mid-December. South China and China are working hard to practice cooperation.

Guangzhou's Situation is a Tragic Decline: Since Mr. Chen Ce and Director Zhang Hui left Guangdong, the situation in Guangzhou has declined sharply. The air and naval forces cannot form teams; only the police remain. Therefore, only four teams participated in the Guangnai Cup. Even the police team, despite having generals such as Li Tiansheng, Tan Jiangbai, and Ye Bi-hua, lost to Lingnan University. There is a sigh that there is no one to promote sports.

Willing to See the China Team: I heard that the Shanghai China team is very strong, with many talents. They will have a friendly match with the Hong Kong team on Sunday. I am very willing to watch and learn about the progress of the Shanghai football scene.

Praising Sports Commentary: The reporter presented several copies of the Sports Commentary Weekly, co-published by many Shanghai sports reporters, and the special issue for this Inter-Port competition. Mr. Mo praised them endlessly, saying that there are few domestic sports publications and that he hopes everyone will do their best to promote them and that he will do his best to introduce them in Hong Kong.

Hong Kong Inter-Port Football Team Chinese Players 202

"From right to left" Sun Kam-shun, Liu Mao, Mo Ying-kui (leader), Wong Mei-shun, Liang Rong-zhao, Zheng Shao-kang (seated) (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Nanjing, 24th: The Ministry of Education has stipulated that the qualifications for sports supervisors or instructors in charge of sports in provinces and cities, in addition to meeting the requirements for civil service appointments, must include graduation from a domestic or foreign university's sports department or sports program and at least two years of service in the sports field. Barro's Opinion on Net Cord Balls 206

= Net Cord Balls are the Most Perfect Shot in Tennis =

= Must Carefully Change Rules of Decades =

丨Reasons Why Net Cord Balls Should Not Be Replayed丨

(London Dispatch) Interest in the proposal to change the current tennis rules continues to increase, but 85% of expert opinions oppose the change.

The opinion of the French veteran Barro is endorsed by all. Barro said,

One of the Tennis Skills: Tennis is a sport where the most perfect shot is a ball that just grazes the net. This is the perfect state that all balls aspire to achieve. Therefore, I do not think it is appropriate to suggest that it should be considered invalid and replayed as a penalty. Moreover, it will cause a lot of disruption in the match. Of course, a net cord ball is a lucky ball, but a match should also have some luck. In short, I believe the current ball rules are very perfect and should be maintained. Rules that have been approved for decades should be changed very carefully. What I am talking about naturally concerns net cord balls during the match, not for the server. For serves, they should be replayed. There are sufficient reasons for replaying a serve that hits the net because the rules stipulate that the receiver cannot attack, so the server can hit the ball arbitrarily between the service line and the net. Therefore, the receiver must stand near the baseline. As a result, balls that hit the net and drop cannot be obtained. In mutual rallies, the receiver can always meet the ball when it crosses the net and return it. If they are at the net, they can also have the opportunity to save most of the net cord balls and also want to have the same kind of return.

Free Talk

Two-in-One Talk

Begging for Help From the League 211

— Zhan Lu

The time for the League of Nations Council to consider the Sino-Japanese dispute is approaching. People sleeping on pillows embroidered with the words "Begging for Help From the League of Nations" are once again dreaming all sorts of good dreams.

Japan's diplomacy is becoming isolated. All countries except Japan do not recognize the existence of Manchukuo! France seems to be clearing away suspicions of siding with Japan, and the United States is implementing recognition of Soviet Russia, giving Japan a major threat. All of these are sweet dreams that are constantly emerging while sleeping on the pillow.

Can the dream become a reality? I don't think so. Even if it becomes a reality, will Japan obey the world's public opinion? I don't think so. Even if we believe that it will obey public opinion, can the Northeast, which has been occupied for many years, be returned to China unconditionally? I don't think so.

Even if we recognize that it will be returned to China unconditionally, can China, which has always relied on others, obtain this good result of begging for help from the League of Nations and then become a rich and strong country? I don't think so.

Instead of begging for help from the League of Nations, it is better to beg for help from "Ourselves United"! What is "Ourselves United"? It is for our own people to unite with each other, put aside private grudges, old grievances, conspiracies, schemes, and other acts of infighting, such as fighting wits, fighting strength, and fighting for cities and territories. Then, no matter how the League of Nations handles the Sino-Japanese dispute, China can always stand in a position of winning without losing. The authority of the words "Ourselves United" is far above the League of Nations. People who like to dream good dreams, quickly put aside this pillow of begging for help from the League of Nations and, at the same time, work together to fully consolidate the work of begging for help from "Ourselves United"!

The two Liu brothers fighting fiercely in Sichuan, looking at the fact that they share the same surname, should unite as one at this time. Don't break our work of "Begging for Help from Ourselves United" and send a gift of "Defaming China" to Matsuoka Yosuke to take to Geneva.

Female Flying General 212

— Xu Tongye

丨Sending Female Aviator Lin Pengxia to Northwest for Investigation丨

Since the September 18th and January 28th incidents, the people of our country deeply know that China's lack of air force is detrimental to national defense. At sea, there is the organization of the China Aviation Construction Association, to awaken the people, its intention is good. Our country's population is large, and the land is vast, being the first in the world, but everything is backward, causing it to be despised by all countries. How can we not sigh? Taking aviation as an example, the United States in 1931 already had 10,635 aircraft and 30,509 pilots, of which women accounted for 510. The United Kingdom is roughly the same. The Northeast has more than 250 aircraft, but it cannot retain one or two, let alone other places. However, China's aviation talent is not completely absent, because there are too many people and too few jobs, and aviation experts have no place to stand. The government has been running aviation for more than 20 years, from Yuan Shikai's hosting of the Nanyuan Aviation School to the present. Apart from purchasing imported aircraft with large sums of money, no other construction work is worth mentioning, which is a great disappointment to the people's expectations. Now, the only female aviator in China, Comrade Lin Pengxia, will have a trip to the Northwest, and various circles are feasting on her every evening. The reason why we express our admiration for this trip of the lady is not because of her amiable personality and outstanding talent, but because the lady was born into a large family and enjoys a life of luxury, so she does not have to travel through mountains and rivers and delve into the provinces of Shaanxi, Gansu, Xinjiang, and Qinghai. Now, the lady can sacrifice material enjoyment, embrace the spirit of fearlessness, and go to the Northwest to investigate alone. Has any Chinese woman ever had such ambitions before? However, this is still not enough. When the lady was studying aviation in the United Kingdom, her flying performance was the best in the entire British female aviation community, making Westerners look sideways and praising her as the Flying General of China. From then on, they did not dare to underestimate the Chinese, so the lady's contribution to the personality of the Chinese nation is truly great. Amy Johnson created a record of British flying, and the government's awards and public propaganda are spared no effort. Although our country is called a semi-colonial country, there are also those who can compare with Amy Johnson, but where is the government's award? Where is the public's propaganda? Although Comrade Lin is a weak woman, her patriotism is far better than that of men. She originally wanted to go to Shanghai to participate in the Anti-Japanese War, but because the peace treaty had been signed, her long-cherished ambition was not fulfilled. However, the Northeast Volunteer Army is still fighting hard, and the Xikang dispute is becoming increasingly acute, with Xinjiang and Qinghai also being affected. Therefore, she decided to go to the Northwest first to investigate the political economy and the people's suffering, and plan the way of development. Her ambition is commendable, and her contribution is great. We only pray for her success and win glory for the country and the nation.

I accidentally learned from a friend in Hangzhou about the death of Ms. Wang Suxiang of the Hangzhou Zhijiang Daily. So, from a state of sorrow and grief, I remembered everything about her life:

Ms. Wang was from Taizhou, Zhejiang. She had a plump figure, thick and wide eyebrows, and thick and large lips, all of which fully expressed her upright nature and courageous spirit. When the Revolutionary Army launched from Guangdong,

Remembering a Female Reporter 213

— Lu Song

She joined the revolutionary work and served as a political trainer in a division headquarters. It is said that she held the rank of a staff officer above a captain. At this time, she fell in love with a comrade, Mr. Xiang Shiyuan, a member of the assembly. Later, they both gave up fighting and devoted themselves to writing, founding the Hangzhou City Daily in Hangzhou. Mr. Xiang became the editor-in-chief, and Ms. Wang became the president. Therefore, Ms. Wang resolutely divorced her husband and declared a formal marriage union with Mr. Xiang.

Ms. Wang was good at speaking and good at socializing. No matter what meeting or group it was, her presence was indispensable. It can truly be said that she attended every meeting and spoke at every meeting. I remember that during the opening of the West Lake Exposition, Shanghai reporters went to Hangzhou together. At the Hangzhou Municipal Government's reception for reporters, Ms. Wang's words were like springs, flowing endlessly. She compared the Shanghai reporters to big birds and the Hangzhou reporters to little birds, which was immediately spread throughout the Shanghai and Hangzhou newspapers. To this day, the classic of "birds" still occupies a page in the story of news reporters.

Ms. Wang was not only good at ordinary socializing but also good at special socializing. The chairman of the Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce, Wang Zhuzhai, was her godfather, and Mr. Meng Lujiu, the former chairman of the Hangzhou Business and People's Association, was also her godfather. As for her own goddaughters, there were too many to count. Ms. Zhou Wenying, a famous socialite who once caused a sensation in the Beijing and Shanghai newspapers, was also one of her goddaughters. Since the Hangzhou Shenbao stopped publication, they continued to run the Zhijiang Daily. Ms. Wang served as the deputy president, running around every day, using her eloquence to raise funds. However, she eventually became exhausted and unable to maintain it. So, she gave the title of president to a Mr. Xu Zhuofu, while Ms. Wang herself abandoned the spirit of running the newspaper and engaged in social work.

Ms. Wang was also a tough woman. She had been involved in several lawsuits for running the newspaper. Once, because of a dispute with the Hangzhou Electric Power Plant, she was jointly sued by the plant for three crimes: theft, defamation, and false accusation. She was detained in Zhejiang's First Prison for several months. When I went to visit her in prison, her haggard face did not diminish her fortitude. Later, thanks to the efforts of Zhuang Songfu, Chen Guofu, Wang Zhuzhai, and other elders, she was safely released from prison.

When the January 28th Incident occurred this year, Ms. Wang organized a Hangzhou Women's Rescue Team and established a branch of the Red Cross in Minhang's Minyuan. She managed it for several months, working hard and without complaint. After returning to Hangzhou, some people said that she had earned more than 10,000 yuan. But according to her own defense, her poor life had not changed.

Now, Ms. Wang has unfortunately died. At least there are several criticisms from people in society about her final conclusion. One is sarcasm with ridicule, and the other is admiration and regret. The former is inevitably harsh, and the latter is too obvious. Overall, I believe that this famous social flower has died too miserably and is pitiful!

After Ms. Wang's death, some people are suggesting building a "Shrine" for her in Fancun, Hang County, and holding regular sacrifices every year. It is expected that if this matter is implemented, then the story of the female hero of the lake and mountains will not be exclusive to Qiu Jin.

Remembering Ye Mingchen 214

— Jin Zhong

丨The Inventor of the Six No's Policy丨

Everyone who has read the history of China for the past hundred years knows that Ye Mingchen was an official who procrastinated and misled the country. He rose from the governor of Guangdong to the governor-general of Liangguang, and was also made a grand academician. His name and position were truly prominent for a time. However, he was a man who liked to brag and was self-conceited. He never took the high-nosed people seriously, so when the Anglo-French Allied Forces first entered Guangdong, he remained calm and indifferent, as if nothing had happened. Although his subordinates repeatedly urged him to seek ways to resist, he only listened to them as "wind in his ears," saying that it would soon subside. When the British army entered Guangzhou, he was unable to defend himself and had to surrender. Fortunately, he still had a thick skin and was not ashamed of being captured. Even though he was exiled to a foreign country (India), he was able to enjoy himself. Sometimes he wrote and painted with people (signing his name as Su Wu of the Sea) to make a living. Later, he died in India. People revered him as the inventor of the Six No's Policy to commemorate his great achievements(?). His Six No's Policy was: 1. No War, 2. No Peace, 3. No Defense, 4. No Death, 5. No Surrender, 6. No Escape. This Six No's Policy was lost for forty or fifty years after his death until the September 18th Northeast Incident occurred last year, when his followers re-implemented them one by one. I think Mr. Ye, if he knew in the afterlife, would cover his face and laugh, saying, "My principles are not isolated!"

Short Message 215

— Yao Zhenya

Ms. Chen Xiujuan, a relative of mine, has been suffering from tuberculosis for many years. Whenever it flares up, her cough and hemoptysis become even more severe, coupled with night sweats and fevers, making it almost unbearable. Recently, I learned that she was introduced by Dr. Zheng, the director of the Changzhou Chengji Hospital, to take the Yijincao from Peisheng Pharmaceutical Company, and she has recovered. It is said that this herb has been proven by famous doctors such as Xia Yingtang, the chairman of the National Federation of Medical and Pharmaceutical Associations, and Xie Liheng, the executive director of the Central National Medical Hall. It is indeed a sacred remedy for the natural cure of pulmonary tuberculosis. The company is located at No. 203 Zhonghua Road, Shanghai. It is recently heard that a North City branch sales office has been established at No. 28 Deyuli, Xikou, Yingda Road.

Dead End 24 216

— Fan Yan

"Cattle herding! Not boasting!" Liu Da sneered coldly. The dinner ended hastily after the debate. Liu Da smoked a dry pipe and went to sleep. Liu's wife continued to peel sunflower seeds under the still dimly lit sky and went to sleep as well. Only A Gen was left and still not sleeping. He knew that even if he went to sleep, he wouldn't be able to fall asleep, so he might as well arrange everything properly first and then go to sleep and sleep more peacefully. When the old couple were both snoring, he quietly went to pack his luggage. This luggage was ridiculously simple because his cotton clothes were still in the pawnshop in Suzhou. He couldn't redeem them until he sold the new rice for money. There was no need to bring summer clothes. There was only a patched cotton vest and a set of shirts and trousers, two pairs of old socks that he had begged from a wealthy family in the city, and nothing else. Thinking of the old saying, "You have to bring small change when you go out," he secretly poured all the banknotes from his mother's pillow into his bag. There were only three silver dollars and four silver coins, which he felt was too little. He also rummaged for a long time in a broken jar under his grandfather's bed and found two banknotes with grains of wheat on them, one a five-yuan note from the Bank of China and the other a one-yuan note from the Bank of Communications. He still remembered that this was the money left over from selling Ai Gu to repay the debt, which was originally prepared to be sent to the clerk of Lawyer Xia but the clerk had kindly returned it to him. Putting them together, he was still short six corners and dozens of cents of the ten dollars. He had already "exhausted his humble resources." He didn't know what the old couple would do if they found out about this great escape tomorrow, would they place an advertisement in the newspaper to arrest him! But he couldn't worry about so much. After packing up, he lay down with his clothes on in his bed in the outer room, still unable to sleep. He heard a rustling sound outside the door and suspected that it was raining. If it rained, it would create more problems. He carefully distinguished that it was not rain but the wind blowing the elm tree outside the door, and the tree leaves and branches were rubbing against the corner of the house. Was it dawn? No, the moonlight was too bright, so he knew that it was the latter half of the night. As the old saying goes, "At twenty-five or six, the moon is at its fullest at the fourth watch."

Liu Da got up early, so A Gen quietly opened the door and went out with his small bag before the sky had fully brightened. He quickened his pace and knocked on Jiang Niupi's door in one breath. Jiang Niupi got up and opened the door, letting him in. His aunt sleepily heated water for him to boil porridge, and after they ate, they said goodbye and went to the lakeside to wait for the sailing boat.

Although the time was different, the position was different, leaving his hometown to change his life was exactly the same as when Ai Gu stood blankly by the lake. A Gen thought, she still had me carrying her small bag, sending her off, asking her "when are you coming back?" What about me? ... He didn't allow himself to think any further! The Suzhou passenger ship, which was good at moving people around and creating a lot of idle gossip, came. A Gen hurriedly picked up his small bag and boarded the ship, unable to turn back to look at his hometown. Until he was far away from Cuiwei Village, he vaguely saw two people standing by the lake in the misty dawn, not knowing if they were grandfather and mother? Because he had also stood by the lake for such a long time, sadly watching Ai Gu's departure.

Financial Bullion Market Remains Strong 218

(Frequent New High Prices) The market yesterday showed a bullish trend again, with slight changes, but the overall trend was good, and new high prices appeared. There were a total of five taels and three mace [unit of weight] of transactions throughout the day. In retrospect, comparing it with the previous afternoon's high of five taels and six mace, the will of the dealers was firm and strong. Initially, it exceeded the 760 tael mark. Although the silver market did not move and the exchange rate fluctuated, it was due to the decline in US dollars and the efforts of the Guangdong merchants to short sell. With the stability of foreign exchange, British pounds and US dollars, the market atmosphere became even more vibrant. It was seen at 67 taels and 8 qian [unit of currency]. Unexpectedly, many long positions were sold off by Fuchang and others, and there were also reports that the US Morgan Company had lent a large number of ounces to the British government. As a result, gold prices turned from strong to weak. Later, there were rumors that war bonds could be used as collateral for currency and stocks, which further fueled the selling frenzy. Finally, it fell to 62 taels and 5 qian. Afterwards, with the exchange rate stabilizing and buying interest remaining strong, the market recovered. All swap transactions were quite active, with Yingfeng Heng and Fuchang swapping with short sellers such as Tong Taichang, Dadecheng, and Ruilian, and the premium ranging from 4 taels and a half to 3 taels and 2 qian. Arrival of British Galvanized Iron is Continuous 231

Hardware trading has been very quiet recently. Apart from a few minor transactions in the city, large-scale deals are still rare. However, market conditions in various cities are thriving due to supply shortages. For example, galvanized iron roofing sheets, new iron wire, iron factory nails, green lead bars, galvanized iron sheets, bamboo-shaped iron, etc., are all showing signs of price increases. The price of British galvanized iron had been rising rapidly due to shallow inventories, but recently, continuous arrivals have created a situation where the standard grade appears strong but is actually weak. The price of thin, patterned sheets is also showing signs of a slight decrease of one or two cents per sheet. Seven-foot sheets are priced at 7.96 taels, and six-foot sheets are priced at 8.2 taels. It is reported that trading is also very slow. However, investigations show that the supply of goods to the market is very extensive, and the price situation is unlikely to return to previous levels.

Supplement to the Shenbao Local Edition

Essay

East and West 253

— Tian Fang

丨Dependence and Independence丨

When discussing the East and the West, a significant difference is the characteristic of dependence versus independence. These two fundamental natures have created two different kinds of people, 丨the weak and the strong.

In the East, there is no shortage of philanthropists who regard giving alms to beggars as the sole virtue, while Western philanthropists do the opposite. A Chinese man and a Western friend once traveled together to Hangzhou. Hangzhou's beggars are famous throughout the land, a special profession beyond the 360 trades. Many poor children are taught begging skills by their parents from a young age, sending them running through the streets. If you travel to Hangzhou, you may find that the only thing spoiling your pleasant mood is the sight of beggars all over the mountains and streets.

At that time, the Chinese man and his Western friend were visiting Lingyin Temple when a child begged from them, following them for half a mile. At first, everyone refused to give anything. However, the Chinese man, being Chinese after all, couldn't bear it and tossed him a copper coin. The Western friend then said, "The lesson I was just teaching him has been ruined by you. This is a lifelong issue, not a matter of a single copper coin. You are harming him, cultivating his dependence, not saving him." His words were filled with regret. The same event, the same concern for the child, reveals the difference in the national character of the East and West. Westerners value "independence," while the East is prone to "dependence."

Looking at material objects, the means of transportation invented in the West are motorcycles and bicycles, while the means of transportation invented in the East are rickshaws, a person-riding-person style. This is a minor matter. More importantly, the weapons used by the West to confront others are "airplanes," "warships," and "tanks," asserting oneself. The weapons used by the East to defend against enemies are "hunger strikes," "telegrams," and "posting slogans," hoping to gain the pity of others. Regardless of whether it concerns a country or a factory, it is questionable whether the "hunger strikes," "telegrams," "posting slogans," and other actions of the weak can achieve victory. Yet, such facts are actually appearing in the political history of the twentieth century. Is this not a manifestation of servility, a disgrace to the East?

Since the fall of the Northeast provinces following the September 18th Incident last year, people in our country have been running around and appealing to the great powers, hoping for assistance, like someone whose house has been robbed and relatives killed, unable to drive away the thieves themselves, and seeking help from neighbors to catch the thieves and recover the stolen goods. There is no such logic in the world. Now, the League of Nations' investigation report has been released, and the conclusion reached is that "China should be jointly administered by the great powers." These blue-eyed and purple-bearded dignitaries would not have the time to completely help our country, so if the great powers do anything, it is for their own benefit. The word "justice" does not exist in the dictionary of the twentieth century. Therefore, the delusive dream of dependence should be awakened. To recover the Northeast and save the nation from disaster, the entire country must abandon the heart of dependence and exert all its strength to confront it directly. As the saying goes, "Heaven helps those who help themselves." Wilson said, "Justice must be backed by force." These words are enough for us to ponder.

The previous "experiments" (according to a certain important figure) have all failed. In the future, we should use real strength to negotiate. Let the authorities know that the country can no longer endure repeated "experiments."

In the Shanghai-Nanjing Train 254

— Wu Tiansheng

Friends and relatives see me off to Jinling Road, intermittent rain reflects on wine cups, long ago I followed hardship to the border, will carry ice and snow to sketch a lifetime, horizontal sky murderous atmosphere above the clouds, hanging dreams train sound drum horns new, the vast world for a cry, crossing the river, the person before my eyes.

Passing Baozi Rock 255

Since the crane's cry disappeared into the white clouds, brocade-like mountains and rivers gave rise to murderous intent. The grass and trees reek of the lingering atmosphere of Daling. The apocalypse of humanity has exhausted Shouyang Mountain. Vainly pitying the Weaver Maid's stifled sobs, how many times have I seen displaced people return with their families. Knowing your efforts to raise your chicks are also bitter, the wave marks forever gnaw at the mossy clothes.

Common Sense

Homemade Fruit Jam 256

— Jiang Xueqin

When we usually eat bread, we must spread fruit jam on it to make it taste better. However, the fruit jam sold on the market, whether it is banana, rose, or other kinds, is very expensive. Even the cheapest goods cost forty or fifty cents. In this way, it is really uneconomical. You must be able to make it yourself to get a large amount of fruit jam without spending a lot of money. Although this is a small skill, it is beneficial to our economy. Moreover, the method of making fruit jam does not require advanced academic theory, nor does it require sophisticated art. Anyone with a little common sense of cooking chemistry can start making it. I have made it several times in practice, and the results have been very satisfactory. If readers are interested, try it according to the method written below, and it will definitely satisfy you.

The method is to first put the bought tomatoes (it is best to use all red ones, but do not be too ripe) into an iron pot, pour an appropriate amount of clean water into the pot, and heat it with fire to make it undergo a chemical reaction. As long as it takes more than ten minutes, its internal flesh will gradually expand, and the outer skin will open by itself. At this time, use an iron ladle to take them out one by one and put them into a white porcelain basin. After they are cold, peel off their skins by hand. Then, put the peeled tomatoes together with the juice flowing out in the porcelain basin back into the iron pot and heat them again. After another ten minutes, put in white sugar (brown sugar is also acceptable) to taste, and at the same time put in a little osmanthus dew to make it slightly fragrant. After putting all these things together, use an iron rod or iron ladle to stir it constantly to make it mix evenly and to prevent it from sticking to the bottom of the pot. When it becomes a thick liquid and turns into a jam color, take it out and seal it in bottles or jars for use.

We only need to use five pounds of tomatoes and one pound of sugar to make five cans of fruit jam. In terms of value, it costs less than half a yuan. Isn't this several times cheaper than buying it on the market? But we must know that those made with white sugar are bright red in color, and those made with brown sugar are purplish-red in color. Adding a little banana dew will turn it into banana fruit jam, and adding a little rose dew will turn it into rose fruit jam. These different points have nothing to do with the nature of the fruit jam itself. The maker can make whichever kind they want.

Speaking of the function of tomato fruit jam, it is not only suitable for the taste. Because these tomatoes contain the most vitamins, we can often eat them to greatly nourish the body and can also treat beriberi and all kinds of dampness and other diseases. This is what we should know.

Turbulence 257

— Wen Bing

He could no longer bear it, so he said to Yi in a very gentle but very depressed tone: "Ruoyan, you must know that people nowadays are not as reliable as you imagine! If you want me to sacrifice, then it's not a problem, as long as he is indeed good, and you can be happy in the future! But I think, he! Kechang, is just such a mediocre man! And Ken you should also think about the history of our love! ··· Ruoyan, think about it calmly!"

After he said these painful words, he lifted his heavy legs, hung his head, and paced back and forth in the room: Ruoyan seemed to be watching his book without feeling anything. The room was dead silent, and the rustling of the wind and the pattering of the rain outside the window were fueling the tide of his heart, as if playing a song of victory, or the low cry of a disappointed person.

He couldn't bear it any longer. This dead silence, so he said again: "Ruoyan, think about it calmly!" He did not wait for Yi's answer, and went out with a large book of manuscripts.

"What's there to think about? Do you want me to die with you!" As soon as his front foot stepped out of the door, Yi finally opened his mouth. This saying was obviously "thorn," no, it was simply like a sharp knife cutting his heart and liver.

Everyone knows, and envy, the beautiful past of Youshi and Ruoyan.

When they were studying at K School in C City, his talent was so superior, and although her knowledge was not very good, she had that graceful and charming figure, and she was considered the school flower in the eyes of the whole school. Because of several contacts at art exhibitions, they went from classmates to friends, and from friends to lovers. When they got married, who didn't say, "A talented man and a beautiful woman, a match made in heaven!" Even they themselves, didn't they yearn for eternal happiness, especially Youshi.

However, the environment was so teasing. When he was in school, although he didn't dare to say what kind of hope he would have in the future, he had never thought that he would have no food to eat, and he had never thought that Ruoyan would change so suddenly! After leaving school, he relied on his hard skills to pursue life and seek a job: but he knew that this ghostly society did not have a place for him at all. After several setbacks, he deeply felt that relying on skills alone was not enough, so he also wanted to learn how to manage like others, but he was, after all, a hard bone, and he couldn't learn how to serve, flatter, and beg others. He would rather starve to death, so he became even poorer, and then the waves of complaining about poverty often stirred up between the couple.

Kechang was their old classmate. He was a famous playboy in school. Not only did Youshi look down on him, but Ruoyan also often said that he was a double-material dandy, naturally not in his eyes, but after he graduated, relying on his brother being the secretary of the ×× government, he effortlessly followed him and became an official, which proved that he was, after all, the winner in the current society.

When Youshi was extremely poor, Kechang suddenly came to see them with a very lavish decoration, and he was very affectionate and very sympathetic. After he left, Ruoyan thought: "Since he is... why not borrow some money from him!" At night, she discussed it with Youshi, who naturally couldn't object, but nodded unnaturally.

That set Kechang's design: "'What is borrowing some money, just take it!'" So Kechang had more opportunities to visit often, so Youshi's family also became familiar, so, so Ruoyan was already Kechang's lover,

Since Ruoyan told Youshi that she had something to do and had to go to N City, after rolling up her clothes and leaving, Youshi only thought she really went to N City. How could he know that one day he went to ×× Hall to collect manuscript fees, when he suddenly met Yi on ×× Road, holding Kechang's hand, running forward as if flying, simply making it impossible for Youshi to catch up and say: "Ruoyan, you are my lover! How can you walk holding Kechang's hand?" He was disappointed, just standing and staring blankly like a wooden chicken.

Later, I don't know if it was because Kechang lost his job and had no money, or for other reasons, Ruoyan was actually trapped in a brothel like a fire pit. Youshi and a friend went to ×× Road to buy something. It was dusk. They were walking and talking while strolling. Suddenly, a woman came diagonally from across the street and grabbed Youshi's sleeve in a panic:

"Dear Youshi! I am your wife! Ruoyan, please forgive me!"

"What, Ruoyan, I really didn't expect to have the opportunity to meet you again! Alas, unfortunately, you are just my past wife!" Youshi forcefully pushed her hand away.

Lecture 258

— Sun Yuan

Originally, there was no need to ring the bell. There were only three people in total, so all you had to do was say "The meeting is starting" and that was it. Why ring the bell? But the school seemed to want to show off its authority and had to ring it once.

The principal ran frantically from the library to the playground, and from the playground to the lecture hall, as if not believing that there were only three people listening to the lecture, and still thinking that maybe someone in the library was reading so intently that they didn't hear the bell, or maybe someone was playing so hard on the playground that they didn't hear the bell clearly, so he went around in a circle.

Obviously, everywhere was quiet. The whole school was asleep today 丨 Sunday.

The three of us sat in the third row, there were four people, and another one was the secretary of the school. The principal dragged him over to "fill the scene." I believe that if our Ah Da丨the tea servant wore a long shirt today, he would definitely be pulled over by the principal to "fill the scene" as well.

The door opened, the principal came in, followed by the Dr. × whose distinguished name we had already seen on the bulletin board.

After the principal introduced him, he distorted the facts and said that the number of people listening to the lecture was small because it was probably due to the impact of this unfortunate incident that happened yesterday. Obviously, a three-year-old child would not believe it.

In fact, to be honest, during normal classes, if they were not happy listening to the lecture, these young masters would take advantage of the professor turning his back to write on the blackboard, lower their heads, bow their bodies, and quickly slip out the door. Those young ladies also raised their tiptoes wearing high heels, and let their hips tremble as they rushed out the door as well.

What's more, today is Sunday. Sunday means "play" day. Who would want to sit here stiffly and listen to boring lectures? The school authorities' attempt to open a lecture on Sunday for the purpose of increasing students' knowledge was obviously a failure.

"It's a pity that these students didn't hear such a good lecture, what a pity! What a pity!" After the lecture, the principal's continuous "pities" expressed his great regret for these students.

"It would be best to change the lecture into a dance party, and then people would come." I said to Mr. × after walking out of the lecture hall.

Really, only by changing the lecture into a dance party will people come!

Movie Special

General Opinion

After Seeing "The President's Dream" at the Guanglu Theater 259

— Da Zai

Yesterday, a friend and I ran to Guanglu to see the new American slapstick film "The President's Dream." The day I saw it was the last day, so at least tens of thousands of people have seen this film in Guanglu and Lanxin before me. I now want to express my opinion, together with the people who have seen this film, that it uses politics as the background and a humorous and satirical style to express the possibility of political corruption.

The plot of this film is roughly like this: Four "political brokers" want to promote Blair, a member of a "warlord family," to become president, but Blair lacks the "talent to deal with the world." Later, a medicine seller came to Washington, probably a wandering quack doctor or the like. And he can speak and sing, his actions are funny, and his appearance and movements are exactly the same as Blair's. So the four political brokers wanted to use him as a "gunman" for the presidential election campaign. As a result, he agreed, and toured the country, returning in triumph. Because Blair's White House dream was about to come true, he wanted to get rid of the "gunman." However, because the two of them looked exactly the same, when Blair ordered his henchmen to tie up the "gunman" and send him to a deserted island in the Arctic Ocean, they accidentally tied up Blair himself. And the "gunman," because things had come to this point, was moved by the patriotic heart of "serving the country and the people," and ascended to the position of president.

It is not surprising that a medicine seller becomes president: The saying goes, generals and ministers are not born of special breeds, and men should strive to improve themselves.

Don't you see that cloth sellers and fish sellers in China have been presidents? But using the parliament building as a backdrop and playing the election scene of the national political conference so vividly is a bit of an insult to the dignity of the government. If it were in our China, the person who made this film would be "guilty and deserving of death." Moreover, making revolutionary martyrs, such as Washington, Lincoln, etc., speak and sing from oil paintings is even more absurd and unforgivable. I don't understand how this film passed the American Film Review Board.

When I was in school, I studied political science, and the books clearly stated the drawbacks of the election system in various countries, how to use the special control of electoral districts and various ingenious methods to make an immoral and capable person gradually become the head of a county or a state. But then they justified themselves, saying that the head of a country is not like this, because the people of a country will never allow such a person to hold a position above all the people. This statement is somewhat contradictory, because the people of a state can tolerate an immoral and intelligent person to be their governor, so why can't the people of a country tolerate it?

If you want to be president, then be president, but you don't have to be coy and say how you are serving the country and the people, which is really scolding all the political activists in the world. The big-nosed one is commendable, because he had to find his top hat that could be flattened among many top hats (top hats), and flattened all the top hats that could not be flattened, and the high hat he flattened was put on high, which also has a very profound meaning. Those who stretch will not be able to stretch again: those who bend can bend and stretch at any time: and can defeat everything and let me show off. Wonderful, wonderful.

Editor's note: The Guanglu's "President's Dream" has already passed, and this article is also a bit of "yesterday's news." But because it is not a film review, but an observation of the film from a political perspective. Originally, movies are a tool for unconscious entertainment, and many "scholars and officials" watched movies and went back to talk to their children, so who would be willing to publish their opinions on watching movies in the newspaper? So I published it according to the general rule of "valuing the few." Not smart.

The Female Lead in "Such a Good Night" 260

Film Review: Impressions of "Tarzan the Ape Man" 261

— Young Fellow

"Tarzan the Ape Man," which caused a sensation with its massive advertisements two months ago, has now returned to Shanghai. Because last time it was exclusively for the wealthy class and young ladies and gentlemen, how could a young fellow like me have such an opportunity?

Around four o'clock, I stepped into the new Rong Guang building. In the darkness and among the crowd, I felt my way to a seat. On the screen was projected "A man lying dead in a pile of ivory." So, I waited for it to finish showing and then watched it again. The story is very ordinary, but the majesty of the African wilderness and the tense and dangerous performances, can one not praise and be amazed? Cliffs and precipices, vast oceans, high mountains and ancient trees... what in nature can be more magnificent and spectacular than these? The desperate struggle between humans and fierce beasts and venomous snakes, cruel, savage, dangerous, and perilous, truly makes the audience break out in a cold sweat! Here, we are given an inspiration. It says: In the fierce competition for survival, only those with resistance can survive. Tarzan has a strong body and powerful muscles, which allow him to wrestle with lions and tigers and win; people must also forge a healthy physique and build a strong nation.

The deepest and most stimulating impression I got was the scene "A man lying dead in a pile of ivory" when I first entered the theater. This scene thoroughly reveals the life of someone who risks everything for greed, telling you "How empty is the dream of gold!" The protagonist in the film, for the sake of greed for ivory, took a great risk and went deep into the terrifying jungle, only to find himself exhausted and dying in the ivory pile after achieving his goal. How unworthy is this! You who somersault in the eyes of money, listen!

If you feel that your life lacks a kind of strength, I advise you not to miss the opportunity, go quickly and get what you seek.

Trends in the Film Industry: Prosperity Cannot Last, Extremes Must Reverse 262

— Star

In the era of silent films, although many people ran from the stage to the screen, there was no significant force. By 1927, things were different. The advent of sound in film gave Broadway performers an excellent opportunity. As a result, people from the stage, like a tide, invaded the film industry. The screen's territory was occupied by them by two-thirds. We have witnessed the decline of many silent film superstars! We have also seen the success of many new stars who have just appeared on the screen. But this year, major changes have occurred again! This is probably a huge reverse trend, right?

This year, not only are a large number of new stars running back to the stage from the screen, but even old stars, staff, directors, set designers, and lighting technicians are leaving Hollywood as if they were crazy. Ernst Lubitsch and Cecil B. DeMille have also signed priority contracts with theaters. When their contracts with Hollywood expire, they may direct stage plays. This is truly a great blessing for theater fans and a great misfortune for film fans. Our future opportunities to appreciate their art will be severely threatened!

A Collection of News from Tianyi Film Company 263

Tianyi Film Company's "Little Actress," starring Yuan Meiyun, is scheduled to premiere at the Rong Guang Grand Theater at the end of this month.

The opera "Poetry on Banana Leaves," starring Wang Renmei, Li Lili, and others at Tianyi, has now been edited and completed and will be released next month.

Since Tianyi began producing sound films last year, there have been rumors of also producing silent films. However, the company has decided not to pursue silent films because the revenue from silent films in various ports is less than one-tenth or one-twentieth of that from sound films, and will focus exclusively on producing sound films.

"Twin Lovebirds in a Sea of Sin," directed by Shao Zuiweng and starring Hu Shan, Ma Loufen, and Shao Suxia, will be completed soon. The new film starring Liming Hui and written by Liming Hui will begin production soon.

Qiu Qixiang, after completing "Little Actress," is preparing to direct a new film "Pursuit" starring Chen Yumei. Qiu recently went to Beijing to scout locations and returned to Shanghai today.

Star Anecdotes: Rockliffe Fellowes' Visit to London 264

— Yan Ming

Everyone Asks Him to Put on His Glasses

Rockliffe Fellowes, the world-renowned comedian, arrived in London on the eighth of last month with his wife.

As he walked through the streets of London, many people shouted at him, "Put on your glasses." Rockliffe responded with a smile. A wave of cheers enveloped them. In reality, Rockliffe's large glasses only had frames and no lenses. But they were used to seeing Rockliffe on the screen. Once they saw Rockliffe without his large glasses appearing on the street, they almost suspected he was an imposter. No wonder Rockliffe said: "I often talk to people who have just come out of the movie theater, because they don't recognize me, so they can be as frank as possible with me about what they think. Sometimes they say Rockliffe is great, sometimes they say Rockliffe is not so good."

On the screen, he is a very natural and lively young man. He rarely talks about his art. According to his own thoughts, his best film should be "Grandma's Boy." The most profitable film, however, is "College." But none of his films don't make money, and sometimes even earn 100% of the original cost.

Rockliffe said he plans to make a film in England, but in the near future, he is prepared to tour Paris, Cannes, etc., and then go to Sweden, perhaps even Russia, and then return to England to spend two weeks seeing England, including his grandfather's hometown of Piraeus, which he left at the age of sixteen.

Rockliffe's latest film, "Movie Crazy," will soon be released in this port. In this film, there are many places that cause maniacal laughter, truly breaking the record of his past films.

Film Industry Investigation: The Art League Company Going to Guangxi 265

— Hong

丨Fifth of the Production Company Visit Notes

Mr. Huang Yicuo, the initiator and host of the Art League Company, said: "The Art League means uniting the artistic circles of the whole country to confront foreign capitalists..." This is the Art League's stance. And what are the production plans for the future? Of course, they will also be developed based on its stance. Therefore, the Art League Company, once established, sent all its personnel in a mighty manner to Guangxi, hoping to leave the greatest page in the history of domestic films: at the same time, it also opens up a new path of light for the current domestic films.

The Art League Company's trip to Guangxi to film has received various material assistance from the Guangxi Provincial Government, and they are also boldly preparing to produce things that have never been seen before in domestic films. This is most worthy of our attention.

Now, according to the reporter's investigation, the Art League's production plans are reported here...

1. "Romance in the Yao Mountains" is being filmed on location deep in the mountains inhabited by the Yao people, with Huang Yunhuan, the Yao prince appointed by the Guangxi Provincial Government, as a guide. 2. "Aerial Romance" has obtained aircraft and other assistance from the Guangxi Civil Aviation Bureau, and when the film is completed, it will open a new record for domestic films. 3. "Black General" and "Ism" are two dramas with strong national colors. 4. "Femme Fatale" is a love film filmed with the scenery of Guilin, known as "the best scenery in the world," as the background. 5. "New Guangxi" is a film with a bit of news nature that systematically introduces Guangxi's scenic spots, cultural relics, mining areas, forest reclamation, and even national defense preparations and construction.

Although the above films are still in production, it is not yet possible to determine whether they will be successful or not. However, the Art League's spirit of enterprise and creation is indeed worthy of being recorded in the history of domestic films. And the personnel of the Art League Company who went to Guangxi, in addition to the old figures in the film industry such as Huang Yicuo, Wang Cilong, and Yang Xiaozhong, the rest, such as Xu Manli, Ye Qingqing, Mei Lin, and Luo Mulan, are all newcomers. Now we are here looking forward to the triumphant return of the Art League Company that went to Guangxi丨

The First Formula of Independent Learning for Film Treatises 269

— Chen Dabei

The best time to practice your eyesight is when the sun first breaks through the dawn, in the place with the cleanest air. But, never throw the baby out with the bathwater, just because your environment does not allow you to have such a suitable time and place, you dare not practice. No matter how unsuitable the environment is, it cannot stop the poor practice and hard practice of those who are determined and powerless, but there are two things that must be paid attention to. First, you should not practice in places where the air is too unclean. Second, you should not practice in places where the light is too insufficient.

When you first start practicing, it is best to use a pencil and put a small black dot between your eyes, in the center of the bridge of your nose. The place where you stand must be about a foot away from the mirror. (It may be slightly farther.) Stand in the attention position in military gymnastics. Your eyes are directly facing the point in the center of the bridge of your nose. First, exhale as much turbid air as possible from your chest, and then slowly inhale a breath of air from your nostrils. The sound of breathing should not be heard by your own ears. When you start to inhale, count "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight" in your mind. When you count to "eight," you have just finished inhaling a breath of air. When you start counting from "one," your eyes only see the point in the center of the bridge of your nose, vaguely and unclearly. Gradually count to "eight," and the eyesight gradually increases. When you count to "eight," the eyesight has gradually progressed from blurred, level vision to attention.

Hold this breath and attentive gaze. Slowly count from "one" to "eight." Then slowly exhale this breath from your nostrils, starting from "one" and counting to "eight." Finish counting eight words and exhale a breath. When you exhale, your eyesight is also gradually decreasing, from attention, level vision, and gradually falling to a blurred and unclear state.

After practicing once, you may rest for a minute and then practice a second time. Beginners should not practice each style more than three times.
